Scan and delete emails, see your next appointment, find recent photos, access most visited web sites, and more, right from your home screen carousel. </p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Pin to front</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">Bring e-mail, photos, or specific apps you use the most to the front of the carousel, where they can be accessed quickly. With a simple swipe or press on the home button, you can also access the familiar app grid, to see the full library of apps on your Fire phone.</p>         </td>     </tr>        </table>  </div>       </td>     </tr> </table>                   <a name="exclusives"></a>              <div class="kmd-section-divider" style="background-image: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/dp/2012/line._V389158116_.gif);"></div>  <table  class="kmd-two-col-container kmd-section-container" style="">     <tr>     <td class="kmd-left-col-container " style="width:510px;">           <img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/dp/2014/S/feature-exclusives-v3._V318871210_.jpg" width="482" class="kmd-side-img" height="655" border="0" />       </td>     <td class="kmd-right-col-container" style="">            <div class="kmd-section-text-container" style="">      <img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/dp/2014/S/s-headline-exclusives._V349400687_.gif" width="662" class="kmd-section-headline" height="135" border="0" />      <div class="kmd-section-tagline">Exclusive Amazon features enhance your watching, listening, and reading. </div>      <table class="kmd-section-text-body">               <tr>     <td style="width:50%; " class="kmd-standard-padding ">          <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">X-Ray for music, video, and books</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">With X-Ray for music, follow along with lyrics for tens of thousands of popular songs, plus get easy-to-access artist information, all with an easy tap or right panel tilt. See IMDb trivia, actor information, plot synopses, and character backgrounds with X-Ray for movies and TV. On books, X-Ray lets you trace characters, places, and ideas as you journey through chapters, using information from Shelfari, YouTube, and Wikipedia.</p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Second Screen</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Start a show on the go and finish it at home with a flick of your finger. Second Screen turns your TV into the primary screen and frees up your Fire phone to provide playback controls, a customized display for X-Ray, or simply be a place to email, browse the web, and more while you watch a movie. Second Screen is available for Amazon Fire TV, PlayStation 3, PlayStation 4, and recent Samsung TVs.</p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Immersion Reading</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">Synchronize the text of your Kindle eBook to its companion Audible audiobook. Real-time highlighting on your Kindle eBook as youre listening helps comprehension, and relieves the strain of reading on the go. Available on thousands of Kindle books and companion Audible audiobooks.</p>                    </td><td style="width:50%;" class="kmd-standard-padding kmd-last-col">         <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">ASAP</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">No more waiting for a video to buffer every time you hit "Play." ASAP (Advanced Streaming and Prediction) learns what movies and shows you like and gets them ready for you to watch. The more you view videos on your Fire phone, the more accurate ASAP becomes, dynamically adapting to your viewing habits.</p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Free backup and restore</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Leveraging the power of Amazon Cloud Drive, Fire  phone can automatically back up device settings, notes, bookmarks, and apps without the need for configuration or connection to a computer, so it's easy to restore your information to a new Fire phone if your device is lost or damaged. </p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Cloud storage for your content</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Fire phone comes with free, unlimited cloud storage, in full resolution, for all photos taken with Fire phone, plus all your Amazon content. Amazon customers also get 5 GB of free personal cloud storage, so you can store your own videos, documents, and other digital content in the cloud, for easy access from all Amazon devices and Cloud Drive.</p>           <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Whispersync</h4>   <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">With Whispersync for Voice, listen to an audiobook on your commute, then automatically pick up where you left off at home, on your Kindle. Whispersync also works across Kindle e-readers and reading apps, Amazon Instant Video, and select GameCircle titles. </p>         </td>     </tr>        </table>  </div>       </td>     </tr> </table>                   <a name="tech"></a>      <div style="display:none;"></div><table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"><tr><td align="center"><map name="tech-details"></map><img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/dp/2014/S/s-headline-techspecs._V351084304_.gif" width="620" align="center" usemap="#tech-details" alt="Technical Details" height="62" border="0" /></td></tr></table>  <table  class="kmd-two-col-container kmd-section-container" style="">     <tr>     <td class="kmd-left-col-container " style="width:510px;">           <img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/dp/2014/S/feature-techspecs-v2._V348722370_.jpg" width="482" class="kmd-side-img" height="1000" border="0" />       </td>     <td class="kmd-right-col-container" style="">            <div class="kmd-technical-details-info"> <table id="technical-details-table" cellspacing="1" cellpadding="10" border="0" width="100%" style="margin-left:0;"> <colgroup> <col style="width: 150px;
